)@@G@@SUBROUTINE  MRSORT(INFIL,OUTFIL,HDRCS,FSTREC,KWPB,BLKFAC,BFR,KAR, @E@@@@KE
)@@G@@     1 EOFAR,KWDS,KYCH,KYLN,NBLKS,NRECS,SEQWD,KFAC,MSGNO,$) @[@@@@C     KF
)@@G@@@E@@@@C         ROUTINE TO EFFICIENTLY SORT LARGE FASTRAND FILES  @[@@@@KG
)@@G@@C     @A@@@@C         A.REQUIREMENTS FOR USE    @G@@@@C           1. FOUKH
)@@G@@R SCRATCH FILES(FASTRAND) MUST BE ASSIGNED TO THE RUN,@G@@@@C           KI
)@@G@@   WITH FILE NAMES TSF1,TSF2,TSF3,AND TSF4.  EACH MUST BE   @E@@@@C     KJ
)@@G@@         LARGE ENOUGH TO HOLD THE ENTIRE SORT FILE.   @[@@@@C     @G@@@@KK
)@@G@@C           2. RECORDS AND BLOCKS MUST CONTAIN AN INTEGRAL NO. OF WORDS KL
)@@G@@@B@@@@C              AND SECTORS RESPECTIVELY.  @[@@@@C     @G@@@@C     KM
)@@G@@      3. THE END OF THE FILE TO BE SORTED MUST BE INDICATED BY A  @E@@@@KN
)@@G@@C              SORT KEY FIELD THAT CONSISTS OF ALL OCTAL 7'S@[@@@@C     KO
)@@G@@@G@@@@C           4. LOGICAL RECORDS ARE CONSIDERED TO BE NUMBERED CONSEKP
)@@G@@CUTIV-@G@@@@C              LY, STARTING WITH ZERO. IF ONE, OR MORE HEADEKQ
)@@G@@R RECORDS   @G@@@@C              ARE TO BE COPIED UNCHANGED TO THE SORTEKR
)@@G@@D FILE, THE VALUES@G@@@@C              OF THE VARIBLES HDRCS(THE NO. OF KS
)@@G@@HEADER RECORDS) AND     @G@@@@C              FSTREC(THE FIRST LOGICAL REKT
)@@G@@CORD TO BE SORTED) MUST BE    @G@@@@C              EQUAL.  IF ONLY THE TKU
)@@G@@OP PART OF THE INPUT FILE IS TO BE  @G@@@@C              SORTED, THE VALKV
)@@G@@UE HDRCS MUST BE ZERO AND FSTREC IS THE   @G@@@@C              LOGICAL RKW
)@@G@@ECORD NO. AT WHICH THE SORT IS TO BEGIN( NOTE:  @G@@@@C              IN KX
)@@G@@THIS CASE, DO NOT ASSIGN THE SAME NAMES TO INFIL AND  @ @@@@C           KY
)@@G@@   OUTFIL !!!).   @[@@@@C     @D@@@@C           5. SORT KEYS MUST BE INTKZ
)@@G@@EGERS OR FIELDATA @[@@@@C     @#@@@@C         B.INPUTS@G@@@@C           LA
)@@G@@1. INFIL  - A 2-WORD ARRAY CONTAINING THE NAME(LJSF) OF THE @C@@@@C     LB
)@@G@@                  INPUT FILE TO BE SORTED @[@@@@C     @G@@@@C           LC
)@@G@@2. OUTFIL - A 2-WORD ARRAY CONTAINING THE NAME(LJSF) OF THE @G@@@@C     LD
)@@G@@                  FILE IN WHICH THE SORTED DATA IS TO BE PLACED   @G@@@@LE
)@@G@@C              AN ASTERISK(LJSF) CAN ALSO BE INPUT IN THIS FIELD, IN    LF
)@@G@@@G@@@@C              WHICH CASE THE NAME OF THE FILE CONTAINING THE SORTLG
)@@G@@ED    @G@@@@C              DATA WILL BE PASSED BACK TO THE CALLING PROGRLH
)@@G@@AM THROUGH  @ @@@@C              THIS ARGUMENT. @[@@@@C     @F@@@@C     LI
)@@G@@      3. HDRCS  - THE NUMBER OF LOGICAL RECORDS TO BE COPIED@G@@@@C     LJ
)@@G@@                  UNCHANGED FROM THE INPUT TO THE OUTPUT FILE     @[@@@@LK
)@@G@@C     @G@@@@C           4. FSTREC - THE LOGICAL RECORD NO.(NUMBERED FROMLL
)@@G@@ ZERO) AT   @D@@@@C                       WHICH THE SORT IS TO BEGIN    LM
)@@G@@@[@@@@C     @B@@@@C           5. WPB    - WORDS PER BLOCK   @[@@@@C     LN
)@@G@@@B@@@@C           6. BLKFAC - BLOCKING FACTOR   @[@@@@C     @G@@@@C     LO
)@@G@@      7. BFR    - THE NAME OF AN ARRAY IN THE CALLING PROGRAM,    @G@@@@LP
)@@G@@C                       DIMENSIONED TO AT LEAST 4 BLOCKS IN LENGTH.     LQ
)@@G@@@[@@@@C     @G@@@@C           8. KAR    - THE NAME OF AN ARRAY IN THE CALR
)@@G@@LLING PROGRAM, OF @G@@@@C                       SUFFICIENT SIZE TO HOLD LS
)@@G@@THE SORT KEY FIELD.     @[@@@@C     @F@@@@C           9. EOFAR  - THE NALT
)@@G@@ME OF ANOTHER ARRAY AS FOR KAR.     @[@@@@C     @G@@@@C          10. KWDLU
)@@G@@S   - THE MINIMUM NUMBER OF WHOLE WORDS(AT 6 CHARACT- @G@@@@C           LV
)@@G@@            ERS/WORD) NEEDED TO CONTAIN THE SORT KEY FIELD. @[@@@@C     LW
)@@G@@@G@@@@C          11. KYCH   - THE STARTING CHARACTER POSITION(STARTING WLX
)@@G@@ITH   @G@@@@C                       ONE) OF THE SORT KEY FIELD IN A LOGILY
)@@G@@CAL RECORD. @[@@@@C     @G@@@@C          12. KYLN   - THE LENGTH(IN CHARLZ
)@@G@@ACTERS) OF THE SORT KEY FIELD.@[@@@@C     @^@@@@C         C.OUTPUTS     MA
)@@G@@@G@@@@C           1. NBLKS  - THE TOTAL NO. BLOCKS REQUIRED BY THE FILE(MB
)@@G@@IN-   @E@@@@C                       CLUDING THE END-OF-FILE INDICATOR). MC
)@@G@@@[@@@@C     @G@@@@C           2. NRECS  - THE TOTAL NO. OF HEADER AND DAMD
)@@G@@TA RECORDS IN THE @G@@@@C                       FILE, NOT COUNTING THE EME
)@@G@@ND-OF FILE INDICATOR    @[@@@@C     @G@@@@C           3. MSGNO  - THE REMF
)@@G@@FERENCE NO. OF AN ERROR MESSAGE. MEANING- @F@@@@C                       MG
)@@G@@FUL ONLY IN THE CASE OF AN ERROR RETURN.  @ @@@@      IMPLICIT INTEGER(AMH
)@@G@@-Z)   @G@@@@      DIMENSION BFR(KWPB,4),PKTS(6,4),KAR(KWDS),EOFAR(KWDS),MI
)@@G@@INFIL(2),   @C@@@@     1 OUTFIL(2),FILES(2,4), SA(4),COU(4),OS(4) @[@@@@MJ
)@@G@@C     @G@@@@      DATA FILES(1,1)/'TSF1  '/,FILES(1,2)/'TSF2  '/,FILES(1MK
)@@G@@,3)/'TSF3  '@ @@@@     1 /,FILES(1,4)/'TSF4  '/ @[@@@@C     @G@@@@      ML
)@@G@@DATA LOEND/O000000000000/,HIEND/O777777777777/,NBLNKS/'      '/   @[@@@@MM
)@@G@@C     @ @@@@      IF(KFAC.LE.1)KFAC=1     @^@@@@      WPB=KWPB/KFAC     MN
)@@G@@@#@@@@      MLT=KFAC    @#@@@@      M=WPB/BLKFAC@A@@@@      IF(WPB.GT.M*MO
)@@G@@BLKFAC)GO TO 930  @A@@@@      IF(KWDS*6.LT.KYLN)GO TO 940   @B@@@@      MP
)@@G@@IF(KYLN.LE.0.OR.KYCH.LE.0)GO TO 940 @#@@@@      MSGNO=0     @#@@@@      MQ
)@@G@@DO 20 I=1,4 @^@@@@      FILES(2,I)=NBLNKS @#@@@@      COU(I)=0    @#@@@@MR
)@@G@@      SA(I)=0     @#@@@@      OS(I)=0     @#@@@@      DO 10 J=1,2 @^@@@@MS
)@@G@@      PKTS(J,I)=NBLNKS  @#@@@@   10 CONTINUE    @#@@@@      DO 20 K=3,6 MT
)@@G@@@#@@@@      PKTS(K,I)=0 @#@@@@   20 CONTINUE    @[@@@@C     @]@@@@      MU
)@@G@@N1=1  @#@@@@      DO 22 I=1,4 @B@@@@      ITST=CHGRTR(INFIL,1,FILES,N1,1MV
)@@G@@2)    @ @@@@      IF(ITST.EQ.0)GO TO 24   @#@@@@      N1=N1+12    @#@@@@MW
)@@G@@   22 CONTINUE    @#@@@@      GO TO 29    @^@@@@   24 IF(I.EQ.1)GO TO 29MX
)@@G@@@]@@@@      N=I-1 @]@@@@      M=N   @#@@@@      DO 26 J=1,N @#@@@@      MY
)@@G@@DO 25 K=1,2 @ @@@@      FILES(K,I)=FILES(K,M)   @#@@@@   25 CONTINUE    MZ
)@@G@@@]@@@@      I=I-1 @]@@@@      M=M-1 @#@@@@   26 CONTINUE    @[@@@@C     NA
)@@G@@@ @@@@      FILES(1,1)=INFIL(1)     @ @@@@      FILES(2,1)=INFIL(2)     NB
)@@G@@@[@@@@C     @#@@@@   29 DO 30 I=1,4 @B@@@@      FLD(18,18,PKTS(5,I))=LOCNC
)@@G@@(BFR(1,I))  @A@@@@      FLD(2,16,PKTS(5,I))=WPB*KFAC  @#@@@@   30 CONTINND
)@@G@@UE    @#@@@@      DO 40 J=1,2 @^@@@@      PKTS(J,1)=INFIL(J)@^@@@@      NE
)@@G@@PKTS(J,2)=INFIL(J)@ @@@@      PKTS(J,3)=FILES(J,3)    @ @@@@      PKTS(JNF
)@@G@@,4)=FILES(J,4)    @#@@@@   40 CONTINUE    @#@@@@      DO 50 K=1,2 @ @@@@NG
)@@G@@      FLD(6,6,PKTS(4,K))=16   @]@@@@      L=K+2 @ @@@@      FLD(6,6,PKTSNH
)@@G@@(4,L))=8    @#@@@@   50 CONTINUE    @#@@@@      KSPB=KWPB/28@^@@@@      NI
)@@G@@SPB=KSPB/KFAC     @A@@@@      IF(28*SPB.NE.WPB)GO TO 900    @^@@@@      NJ
)@@G@@WPR=WPB/BLKFAC    @#@@@@      CPR=WPR*6   @#@@@@      NWDS=KYLN/6 @^@@@@NK
)@@G@@      NCH=KYLN-NWDS*6   @ @@@@      IF(NWDS.LT.1)GO TO 70   @^@@@@      NL
)@@G@@DO 60 I=1,NWDS    @#@@@@      KAR(I)=LOEND@^@@@@      EOFAR(I)=HIEND    NM
)@@G@@@#@@@@   60 CONTINUE    @ @@@@   70 IF(NCH.LT.1)GO TO 75    @#@@@@      NN
)@@G@@N1=NWDS*6+1 @B@@@@      CALL CHMOVE(LOEND,1,KAR,N1,NCH)     @B@@@@      NO
)@@G@@CALL CHMOVE(HIEND,1,EOFAR,N1,NCH)   @D@@@@   75 IF(HDRCS.NE.0.AND.HDRCS.NP
)@@G@@NE.FSTREC)GO TO 910     @]@@@@      IBRN=1@]@@@@      SW1=0 @]@@@@   80 NQ
)@@G@@A=1   @]@@@@      B=2   @]@@@@      C=3   @]@@@@      D=4   @]@@@@   85 NR
)@@G@@INT=0 @[@@@@C     @]@@@@      OUT=C @ @@@@      IF(HDRCS.EQ.0)GO TO 130 NS
)@@G@@@^@@@@      STT=IOD(PKTS(1,A))@A@@@@      HDBLKS=HDRCS/(BLKFAC*KFAC)    NT
)@@G@@@B@@@@      PLSRCS=HDRCS-HDBLKS*BLKFAC*KFAC     @ @@@@      IF(HDBLKS.LTNU
)@@G@@.1)GO TO 110@^@@@@      DO 100 KK=1,HDBLKS@A@@@@      CALL GIOCK(PKTS(1,NV
)@@G@@A),IST,$88) @#@@@@      GO TO 89    @ @@@@   88 IF(IST.NE.5)GO TO 920   NW
)@@G@@@^@@@@   89 DO 90 KJ=1,KWPB   @ @@@@      BFR(KJ,C)=BFR(KJ,A)     @#@@@@NX
)@@G@@   90 CONTINUE    @^@@@@      STT=IOD(PKTS(1,C))@ @@@@      SA(A)=SA(A)+NY
)@@G@@SPB*KFAC    @A@@@@      FLD(12,24,PKTS(6,A))=SA(A)    @^@@@@      STT=IONZ
)@@G@@D(PKTS(1,A))@ @@@@      SA(C)=SA(C)+SPB*KFAC    @A@@@@      CALL GIOCK(POA
)@@G@@KTS(1,C),IST,$920)@A@@@@      FLD(12,24,PKTS(6,C))=SA(C)    @#@@@@  100 OB
)@@G@@CONTINUE    @A@@@@      COU(A)=HDBLKS*BLKFAC*KFAC     @A@@@@      COU(C)OC
)@@G@@=HDBLKS*BLKFAC*KFAC     @A@@@@  110 CALL GIOCK(PKTS(1,A),IST,$112)@#@@@@OD
)@@G@@      GO TO 113   @ @@@@  112 IF(IST.NE.5)GO TO 920   @ @@@@  113 IF(PLSOE
)@@G@@RCS.LT.1)GO TO 150@^@@@@      PWDS=PLSRCS*WPR   @[@@@@C     @^@@@@      OF
)@@G@@DO 120 KK=1,PWDS  @ @@@@      BFR(KK,C)=BFR(KK,A)     @#@@@@  120 CONTINOG
)@@G@@UE    @#@@@@      OS(A)=PLSRCS@ @@@@      COU(A)=COU(A)+PLSRCS    @ @@@@OH
)@@G@@      COU(C)=COU(C)+PLSRCS    @#@@@@      OS(C)=PLSRCS@#@@@@      GO TO OI

)@@G@@  0  325  30   1.0211E-0*[@@@@*SDFF*@[@@@@/.    @E@@@@.                 EV
)@@G@@     *********************************    @E@@@@.                      *EW
)@@G@@    THE SAVESECURE PROCESSOR   *    @E@@@@.                      *      EX
)@@G@@     WRITTEN BY          *    @E@@@@.                      * BOB RUSSUM EY
)@@G@@AND KAREN DELOUCHE *    @E@@@@.                      * MISSISSIPPI STATEEZ
)@@G@@ UNIVERSITY  *    @E@@@@.                      *        COMPUTER CENTER FA
)@@G@@       *    @E@@@@.                      *        JANUARY 10, 1975      FB
)@@G@@ *    @E@@@@.                      *********************************    FC
)@@G@@@[@@@@.     @[@@@@.     @I@@@@.      THE SAVESECURE PROCESSOR IS A PROGRFD
)@@G@@AM DESIGNED TO SAVE AS MUCH CONTENT AS    @H@@@@. POSSIBLE FROM A SECUREFE
)@@G@@ TAPE IN POOR CONDITION.  THE PROCESSOR READS THE TAPE@I@@@@. AND BUILDSFF
)@@G@@ A COPY OF IT WHICH IS SATISFACTORY FOR USE BY THE SECURE PROCESSOR.    FG
)@@G@@@G@@@@. THE NEW TAPE CONTAINS ALL THE FILES THAT WERE IN GOOD CONDITION FH
)@@G@@ON THE@I@@@@. ORIGINAL TAPE.  HOWEVER, IT DOES NOT CONTAIN THE FILES WHIFI
)@@G@@CH WERE IN UNSATIS-     @H@@@@. FACTORY CONDITION (BECAUSE OF BAD HEADERFJ
)@@G@@ LABELS, PARITY, ETC.).  THEREFORE, @D@@@@. THESE FILES MUST BE RESTOREDFK
)@@G@@ FROM ANOTHER TAPE.     @G@@@@.      NOTE:  THE RESTORED FILES MUST BE WFL
)@@G@@RITTEN INTO IN ORDER THAT NEW @H@@@@. BACKUPS WILL BE MADE OF THEM.  IF FM
)@@G@@THE FILE IS A PROGRAM FILE, THIS MAY BE   @H@@@@. ACCOMPLISHED BY PACKINFN
)@@G@@G AND PREPPING THE FILE.  IF IT IS A DATA FILE, IT MAY@F@@@@. BE ACCOMPLFO
)@@G@@ISHED BY UPDATING THE FILE IN THE FOLLOWING MANNER:   @H@@@@. @DATA Q*F.FP
)@@G@@,Q*F. (WILL COPY THE FILE INTO ITSELF).   IF THE FILE IS NEITHER A@H@@@@FQ
)@@G@@. PROGRAM FILE NOR A FILE IN SDF FORMAT, THEN IT MAY BE NECESSARY TO PROFR
)@@G@@DUCE A@#@@@@. NEW F-CYCLE.    @[@@@@.     @[@@@@.     @H@@@@.      THEREFS
)@@G@@ ARE TWO MODES OF OPERATION OF THE SAVESECURE PROCESSOR.  IN ONE  @H@@@@FT
)@@G@@. MODE, THE PROCESSOR DUMPS THE CONTENTS OF THE SECURE TAPE IN OCTAL FORFU
)@@G@@MAT.  @I@@@@. THIS MODE MAY BE USED TO EXAMINE SELECTED CONTENTS OF THE FV
)@@G@@TAPE.  IN THE OTHER     @H@@@@. MODE, THE PROCESSOR READS THE TAPE AND SFW
)@@G@@UPPLIES INFORMATION ABOUT THE CONDI-@H@@@@. TION OF THE FILES THAT ARE BFX
)@@G@@ACKED-UP ON IT.  IN THIS MODE, THE PROCESSOR CAN@I@@@@. OPTIONALLY PRODUFY
)@@G@@CE A COPY OF THE SECURE TAPE THAT IS IN SATISFACTORY CONDITION    @A@@@@FZ
)@@G@@. FOR USE BY THE SECURE PROCESSOR.  @[@@@@.     @[@@@@.     @H@@@@.     GA
)@@G@@ THE PROCESSOR CALL TO THE SAVESECURE PROCESSOR OPERATING IN THE FIRST  GB
)@@G@@@^@@@@. MODE IS AS FOLLOWS:   @B@@@@.           @SAVESECURE,D SPEC1,SPECGC
)@@G@@2     @H@@@@. THE 'D' OPTION INDICATES THAT THE CONTENTS OF THE TAPE AREGD
)@@G@@ TO BE DUMPED.    @A@@@@. SPEC1 AND SPEC2 ARE EACH OPTIONAL.@I@@@@.     GE
)@@G@@ SPEC1 IS A DECIMAL NUMBER INDICATING THE NUMBER OF BLOCKS OF THE TAPE TGF
)@@G@@O     @C@@@@. BE DUMPED.  THE DEFAULT VALUE IS 200 BLOCKS.  @I@@@@.     GG
)@@G@@ SPEC2 IS A DECIMAL NUMBER INDICATING THE NUMBER OF WORDS PER BLOCK TO BGH
)@@G@@E     @D@@@@. DUMPED.  THE DEFAULT VALUE IS 8 WORDS PER BLOCK.    @H@@@@GI
)@@G@@.      IN THIS MODE, THE SECURE TAPE MUST BE ASSIGNED WITH THE FILENAME GJ
)@@G@@'OLD'.@[@@@@.     @[@@@@.     @H@@@@.      THE PROCESSOR CALL TO THE SAVGK
)@@G@@ESECURE PROCESSOR OPERATING IN THE SECOND @^@@@@. MODE IS AS FOLLOWS:   GL
)@@G@@@^@@@@.           @SAVESECURE @H@@@@. THE CHOICE OF WHETHER OR NOT TO PRGM
)@@G@@ODUCE A COPY OF THE TAPE IS DETERMINED BY @F@@@@. THE RESPONSE TO A MESSGN
)@@G@@AGE WHICH APPEARS ON THE SYSTEM CONSOLE.  @I@@@@.      IN THIS MODE, THEGO
)@@G@@ ORIGINAL SECURE TAPE MUST BE ASSIGNED WITH THE FILENAME    @H@@@@. 'OLDGP
)@@G@@', AND THE COPY (IF THE COPY OPTION IS TAKEN) WITH THE FILENAME 'NEW'.  GQ
)@@G@@@[@@@@/.    @C@@@@. THE FORMAT OF SECURE TAPES IS AS FOLLOWS:     @[@@@@GR
)@@G@@.     @[@@@@.     @E@@@@          .                           HEADER BLOGS
)@@G@@CK OF TAPE  @H@@@@          .         ..................................GT
)@@G@@.....................   @H@@@@          . 0       :                     GU
)@@G@@  'SECURE'                      :   @H@@@@          .         :.........GV
)@@G@@............................................:   @H@@@@          . 1     GW
)@@G@@  :                       '*TAPE*'                      :   @H@@@@      GX
)@@G@@    .         :.....................................................:   GY
)@@G@@@H@@@@          . 2       :                       SITE ID               GZ
)@@G@@        :   @H@@@@          .         :.................................HA
)@@G@@....................:   @H@@@@          . 3       :                     HB
)@@G@@   RUN ID                       :   @H@@@@          .         :.........HC
)@@G@@............................................:   @H@@@@          . 4     HD
)@@G@@  :                     REEL NUMBER                     :   @H@@@@      HE
)@@G@@    .         :.....................................................:   HF
)@@G@@@H@@@@          . 5       :              PREVIOUS REEL NO.(IF ANY)      HG
)@@G@@        :   @H@@@@          .         :.................................HH
)@@G@@....................:   @H@@@@          . 6       :     REL. REEL   :   HI
)@@G@@ 0   :           010101         :   @H@@@@          .         :.........HJ
)@@G@@............................................:   @H@@@@          . 7     HK
)@@G@@  :                        ZEROES                       :   @H@@@@      HL
)@@G@@    .         /                                                     /   HM
)@@G@@@H@@@@          .         /                                             HN
)@@G@@        /   @H@@@@          . 063     :                                 HO
)@@G@@                    :   @H@@@@          .         :.....................HP
)@@G@@................................:   @[@@@@.     @[@@@@.     @F@@@@      HQ
)@@G@@    .                     HEADER BLOCK OF FILE(1800 WORDS)  @H@@@@      HR
)@@G@@    .         :.....................................................:   HS
)@@G@@@H@@@@          . 0       :                       'SECURE'              HT
)@@G@@        :   @H@@@@          .         :.................................HU
)@@G@@....................:   @H@@@@          . 1       :                     HV
)@@G@@  '*FILE*'                      :   @H@@@@          .         :.........HW
)@@G@@............................................:   @H@@@@          . 2     HX
)@@G@@  :                        RUN ID                       :   @H@@@@      HY
)@@G@@    .         :.....................................................:   HZ
)@@G@@@H@@@@          . 3       :                     REEL NUMBER             IA
)@@G@@        :   @H@@@@          .         :.................................IB
)@@G@@....................:   @H@@@@          . 4       :               TIME AIC
